 duusare din 'sahitya ajtak' ke 'hallaa bol' manch par 'vichaardhaara kaa sahitya' seshan main sudhish pachori (lekhak), sachchidanand joshi (sadsy sachiv, indira gandhi rashtriya kala centre) or anant vijay (lekhak, aalochak) ne apni raay rakhi

 Among them, Vijay Joshi has been fined 25 lakh with a sentence of three years, AK Basu has been fined one lakh while giving a sentence of three years
